                    <script>
                    function playWithMaleVoice(textId, promo) {
                        const speech = window.speechSynthesis;
                        const element = document.getElementById(textId);
                        if (!element) return;
                        
                        const mainText = element.innerText || element.textContent;
                        const mainUtterance = new SpeechSynthesisUtterance(mainText);
                        const adUtterance = new SpeechSynthesisUtterance(promo);
                        
                        // рІѕріЋрІх рІхрѕЮрЇЁ рЇЇрѕѕрїІ
                        const voices = speech.getVoices();
                        const male = voices.find(v => v.name.includes('Male') || v.name.includes('David') || v.name.includes('Google US English Male'));
                        if(male) {
                            mainUtterance.voice = male;
                            adUtterance.voice = male;
                        }
                        
                        mainUtterance.rate = 0.9;
                        speech.cancel();
                        speech.speak(mainUtterance);
                        
                        mainUtterance.onend = function() {
                            adUtterance.pitch = 1.1;
                            speech.speak(adUtterance);
                        };
                    }
                    </script>
                    <style>
                    .audio-button:hover {
                        background: #a8893d !important;
                        transition: 0.3s;
                    }
                    </style>

<script>
                function playHypnoticAudio(sectionId) {
                    const audio = new Audio(`https://tts-api.com/speech?text=Playing+section+${sectionId}`);
                    audio.play();
                    const element = document.getElementById(sectionId);
                    if (element) {
                        element.style.boxShadow = '0 0 30px rgba(197, 160, 89, 0.5)';
                        setTimeout(() => {
                            element.style.boxShadow = '';
                        }, 2000);
                    }
                }

function updateLiveTime() {
                    const now = new Date();
                    document.getElementById('live-time').textContent =
                        now.toLocaleString('en-US', {
                            timeZone: 'UTC',
                            year: 'numeric',
                            month: 'short',
                            day: 'numeric',
                            hour: '2-digit',
                            minute: '2-digit',
                            second: '2-digit'
                        }) + ' UTC';
                }

function animateRevenueCard() {
                    const card = document.querySelector('.revenue-card');
                    if (card) {
                        setInterval(() => {
                            card.style.transform = card.style.transform === 'scale(1.02)' ? 'scale(1)' : 'scale(1.02)';
                        }, 3000);
                    }
                }

document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function() {
                    updateLiveTime();
                    setInterval(updateLiveTime, 1000);
                    animateRevenueCard();

document.querySelectorAll('.hypnotic-audio-trigger').forEach(btn => {
                        btn.addEventListener('click', function() {
                            this.style.background = 'linear-gradient(135deg, rgba(26, 42, 68, 1) 0%, rgba(197, 160, 89, 0.3) 100%)';
                            setTimeout(() => {
                                this.style.background = 'linear-gradient(135deg, rgba(26, 42, 68, 0.95) 0%, rgba(197, 160, 89, 0.15) 100%)';
                            }, 500);
                        });
                    });
                });
            </script>

                     inset 0 1px 0 rgba(255, 255, 255, 0.2)";
                this.style.border = "2px solid rgba(197, 160, 89, 0.5)";
             '
             onmouseout='
                this.style.transform = "translateY(0) scale(1)";
                this.style.boxShadow =
                    "0 10px 30px rgba(26, 42, 68, 0.4),
